The Face cards which are kings, queens and jacks are counted as 10 points. The dealer and the player count an ace as 1 point or 11 points, and all other cards are counted according to the numeric value shown on the card. The players after receiving their first two cards, have an option of getting a hit or taking an additional card. The player or the dealer wins by having a score of 21 or by having the higher score that is less than 21. Having a score higher than 21 is going bust or called busting which will result in a loss.
